0-2s - maybe calm but the model turned over the had so there can be some signal
3-7s - 4 fingers (except thumb i mean) close/open many times (exactly 7 times)
8s - calm
9-11s - tumb open/close 4 times
12 - 18s - open close 4 fingers (+ slight moves of thumb) 6 times
19s - calm
20-25s - 4 fingers open/close
26-27s - end of the experiment, useless moves
